# OCSF Schema Documentation

**Source:** SentinelOne Customer Community Knowledge Base  
**Overview article:** https://community.sentinelone.com/s/article/000010516  
**Compiled:** Auto-extracted summary (per-article field-name lists)

## About OCSF

The Open Cybersecurity Schema Framework (OCSF) is an open-source standard that provides a structured schema for representing security events. SentinelOne uses OCSF field definitions in its Singularity Data Lake (SDL) Event Search and PowerQuery (S1QL 2.0).

The documentation is organized into seven subsection topics, each covering one OCSF event category. Individual event types are split across multiple "Part N" articles because the schemas contain hundreds of fields each. The sections below list every article, its URL, and the field-name list extracted from it. Field counts of exactly 300 indicate the article presents a paginated slice of a larger field set; the remaining fields for that event appear in the subsequent "Part N" article(s).

## Summary Statistics

- **Total subsection topics:** 7
- **Total articles documented:** 96
- **Total field entries extracted:** 25759

1. [System Activity](#system-activity)

7. [Unified Alert Management](#unified-alert-management)

## Notes and Caveats

- Field lists were extracted programmatically from tables on each article page. The per-article field cap of 300 corresponds to a pagination limit used by the source documentation; when an event category has more than 300 fields, the schema is split across sequentially numbered "Part N" articles.
- Full descriptions, data types, and enum valid values for each field are available on the source article URLs and are not reproduced in this document to respect copyright.
- For authoritative reference, consult the live SentinelOne Knowledge Base articles via the URLs listed under each entry.
